Updating the\n491:         input partitions of tasks also updates the mapping from source nodes to input topics in the processor topology\n492:         within the task. The mapping is updated with the topics from the topology metadata. The topology metadata does\n493:         not prefix intermediate internal topics with the application ID. Thus, if a standby task has input partitions\n494:         from an intermediate internal topic the update of the mapping in the processor topology leads to an invalid\n495:         topology exception during recycling of a standby task to an active task when the input queues are created. It takes two maps (active and standby task IDs to their topic partitions) as input and performs the following reconciliation logic: (1) logs the delta between existing and new assignments, (2) registers subscribed topics from new active partitions, (3) prepares mutable copies of assignment maps and empty collections for recycling/closing tasks, (4) locks tasks appearing in both old and new assignments to prevent concurrent modifications, (5) iterates over all existing tasks - updating input partitions and resuming if already active, marking for recycling if changing between active/standby roles, or marking for clean closure if no longer assigned, (6) closes and recycles marked tasks, (7) unlocks previously locked tasks, (8) aggregates exceptions with priority (fatal > migrated > corrupted), and (9) creates brand-new tasks for any remaining IDs in the assignment maps.
